\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{/*****************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ sc\_signed.h\ -\/-\/\ Arbitrary\ precision\ signed\ arithmetic.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ This\ file\ includes\ the\ definitions\ of\ sc\_signed\_bitref,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ sc\_signed\_subref,\ and\ sc\_signed\ classes.\ The\ first\ two\ classes\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ proxy\ classes\ to\ reference\ one\ bit\ and\ a\ range\ of\ bits\ of\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ sc\_signed\ number,\ respectively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ An\ sc\_signed\ number\ has\ the\ sign-\/magnitude\ representation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ internally.\ However,\ its\ interface\ guarantees\ a\ 2's-\/complement}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ representation.\ The\ sign-\/magnitude\ representation\ is\ chosen}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ because\ of\ its\ efficiency:\ The\ sc\_signed\ and\ sc\_unsigned\ types\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ optimized\ for\ arithmetic\ rather\ than\ bitwise\ operations.\ For}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ arithmetic\ operations,\ the\ sign-\/magnitude\ representation\ performs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ better.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ The\ implementations\ of\ sc\_signed\ and\ sc\_unsigned\ classes\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ almost\ identical:\ Most\ of\ the\ member\ and\ friend\ functions\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ defined\ in\ sc\_nbcommon.cpp\ and\ sc\_nbfriends.cpp\ so\ that\ they\ can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ be\ shared\ by\ both\ of\ these\ classes.\ These\ functions\ are\ chosed\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ defining\ a\ few\ macros\ before\ including\ them\ such\ as\ IF\_SC\_SIGNED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ and\ CLASS\_TYPE.\ Our\ implementation\ choices\ are\ mostly\ dictated\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ performance\ considerations\ in\ that\ we\ tried\ to\ provide\ the\ most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ efficient\ sc\_signed\ and\ sc\_unsigned\ types\ without\ compromising}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ their\ interface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ For\ the\ behavior\ of\ operators,\ we\ have\ two\ semantics:\ the\ old\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ new.\ The\ most\ important\ difference\ between\ these\ two\ semantics\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ that\ the\ old\ semantics\ is\ closer\ to\ C/C++\ semantics\ in\ that\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ result\ type\ of\ a\ binary\ operator\ on\ unsigned\ and\ signed\ arguments}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ is\ unsigned;\ the\ new\ semantics,\ on\ the\ other\ hand,\ requires\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ result\ type\ be\ signed.\ The\ new\ semantics\ is\ required\ by\ the\ VSIA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ C/C++\ data\ types\ standard.\ We\ have\ implemented\ the\ new\ semantics.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Original\ Author:\ Ali\ Dasdan,\ Synopsys,\ Inc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *****************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ \textcolor{comment}{/*****************************************************************************}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01375\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01376\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ The\ comparison\ of\ the\ old\ and\ new\ semantics\ are\ as\ follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01377\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01378\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ Let\ s\ =\ sc\_signed,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01379\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ u\ =\ sc\_unsigned,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01380\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ un\ =\ \{\ uint64,\ unsigned\ long,\ unsigned\ int\ \},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01381\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ sn\ =\ \{\ int64,\ long,\ int,\ char*\ \},\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01382\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ OP\ =\ \{\ +,\ -\/,\ *,\ /,\ \%\ \}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01383\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01384\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ Old\ semantics:\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ New\ semantics:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01385\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ u\ OP\ u\ -\/>\ u\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ u\ OP\ u\ -\/>\ u}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01386\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ s\ OP\ u\ -\/>\ u\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ s\ OP\ u\ -\/>\ s}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01387\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ u\ OP\ s\ -\/>\ u\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ u\ OP\ s\ -\/>\ s}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01388\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ s\ OP\ s\ -\/>\ s\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ s\ OP\ s\ -\/>\ s}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01389\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01390\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ u\ OP\ un\ =\ un\ OP\ u\ -\/>\ u\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ u\ OP\ un\ =\ un\ OP\ u\ -\/>\ u}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01391\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ u\ OP\ sn\ =\ sn\ OP\ u\ -\/>\ u\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ u\ OP\ sn\ =\ sn\ OP\ u\ -\/>\ s}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01392\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01393\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ s\ OP\ un\ =\ un\ OP\ s\ -\/>\ s\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ s\ OP\ un\ =\ un\ OP\ s\ -\/>\ s}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01394\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ s\ OP\ sn\ =\ sn\ OP\ s\ -\/>\ s\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ s\ OP\ sn\ =\ sn\ OP\ s\ -\/>\ s}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01395\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01396\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ In\ the\ new\ semantics,\ the\ result\ is\ u\ if\ both\ operands\ are\ u;\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01397\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ result\ is\ s\ otherwise.\ The\ only\ exception\ is\ subtraction.\ The\ result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01398\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ of\ a\ subtraction\ is\ always\ s.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01399\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01400\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ The\ old\ semantics\ is\ like\ C/C++\ semantics\ on\ integer\ types;\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01401\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ new\ semantics\ is\ due\ to\ the\ VSIA\ C/C++\ data\ types\ standard.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01402\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01403\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01404\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ARITHMETIC\ OPERATORS:}}
